   72 import Data.Char (ord)
   73 import qualified Data.Bits

   75 -- | Encode a Haskell String to a list of Word8 values, in UTF8 format.
   76 utf8Encode :: Char -> [Word8]
   77 utf8Encode = uncurry (:) . utf8Encode'
   78 
   79 utf8Encode' :: Char -> (Word8, [Word8])
   80 utf8Encode' c = case go (ord c) of
   81                   (x, xs) -> (fromIntegral x, map fromIntegral xs)
   82  where
   83   go oc
   84    | oc <= 0x7f       = ( oc
   85                         , [
   86                         ])
   87 
   88    | oc <= 0x7ff      = ( 0xc0 + (oc `Data.Bits.shiftR` 6)
   89                         , [0x80 + oc Data.Bits..&. 0x3f
   90                         ])
   91 
   92    | oc <= 0xffff     = ( 0xe0 + (oc `Data.Bits.shiftR` 12)
   93                         , [0x80 + ((oc `Data.Bits.shiftR` 6) Data.Bits..&. 0x3f)
   94                         , 0x80 + oc Data.Bits..&. 0x3f
   95                         ])
   96    | otherwise        = ( 0xf0 + (oc `Data.Bits.shiftR` 18)
   97                         , [0x80 + ((oc `Data.Bits.shiftR` 12) Data.Bits..&. 0x3f)
   98                         , 0x80 + ((oc `Data.Bits.shiftR` 6) Data.Bits..&. 0x3f)
   99                         , 0x80 + oc Data.Bits..&. 0x3f
  100                         ])
  101 
  102 #endif
  103 
  104 type Byte = Word8
  105 
  106 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  107 -- The input type
  108 
  109 #if defined(ALEX_POSN) || defined(ALEX_MONAD) || defined(ALEX_GSCAN)
  110 type AlexInput = (AlexPosn,     -- current position,
  111                   Char,         -- previous char
  112                   [Byte],       -- pending bytes on current char
  113                   String)       -- current input string
  114 
  115 ignorePendingBytes :: AlexInput -> AlexInput
  116 ignorePendingBytes (p,c,_ps,s) = (p,c,[],s)
  117 
  118 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
  119 alexInputPrevChar (_p,c,_bs,_s) = c
  120 
  121 alexGetByte :: AlexInput -> Maybe (Byte,AlexInput)
  122 alexGetByte (p,c,(b:bs),s) = Just (b,(p,c,bs,s))
  123 alexGetByte (_,_,[],[]) = Nothing
  124 alexGetByte (p,_,[],(c:s))  = let p' = alexMove p c
  125                               in case utf8Encode' c of
  126                                    (b, bs) -> p' `seq`  Just (b, (p', c, bs, s))
  127 #endif
  128 
  129 #if defined(ALEX_POSN_BYTESTRING) || defined(ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING)
  130 type AlexInput = (AlexPosn,     -- current position,
  131                   Char,         -- previous char
  132                   ByteString.ByteString,        -- current input string
  133                   Int64)           -- bytes consumed so far
  134 
  135 ignorePendingBytes :: AlexInput -> AlexInput
  136 ignorePendingBytes i = i   -- no pending bytes when lexing bytestrings
  137 
  138 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
  139 alexInputPrevChar (_,c,_,_) = c
  140 
  141 alexGetByte :: AlexInput -> Maybe (Byte,AlexInput)
  142 alexGetByte (p,_,cs,n) =
  143     case ByteString.uncons cs of
  144         Nothing -> Nothing
  145         Just (b, cs') ->
  146             let c   = ByteString.w2c b
  147                 p'  = alexMove p c
  148                 n'  = n+1
  149             in p' `seq` cs' `seq` n' `seq` Just (b, (p', c, cs',n'))
  150 #endif
  151 
  152 #ifdef ALEX_BASIC_BYTESTRING
  153 data AlexInput = AlexInput { alexChar :: {-# UNPACK #-} !Char,      -- previous char
  154                              alexStr ::  !ByteString.ByteString,    -- current input string
  155                              alexBytePos :: {-# UNPACK #-} !Int64}  -- bytes consumed so far
  156 
  157 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
  158 alexInputPrevChar = alexChar
  159 
  160 alexGetByte (AlexInput {alexStr=cs,alexBytePos=n}) =
  161     case ByteString.uncons cs of
  162         Nothing -> Nothing
  163         Just (c, rest) ->
  164             Just (c, AlexInput {
  165                 alexChar = ByteString.w2c c,
  166                 alexStr =  rest,
  167                 alexBytePos = n+1})
  168 #endif
  169 
  170 #ifdef ALEX_STRICT_BYTESTRING
  171 data AlexInput = AlexInput { alexChar :: {-# UNPACK #-} !Char,
  172                              alexStr :: {-# UNPACK #-} !ByteString.ByteString,
  173                              alexBytePos :: {-# UNPACK #-} !Int}
  174 
  175 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
  176 alexInputPrevChar = alexChar
  177 
  178 alexGetByte (AlexInput {alexStr=cs,alexBytePos=n}) =
  179     case ByteString.uncons cs of
  180         Nothing -> Nothing
  181         Just (c, rest) ->
  182             Just (c, AlexInput {
  183                 alexChar = ByteString.w2c c,
  184                 alexStr =  rest,
  185                 alexBytePos = n+1})
  186 #endif
  187 
  188 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  189 -- Token positions
  190 
  191 -- `Posn' records the location of a token in the input text.  It has three
  192 -- fields: the address (number of characters preceding the token), line number
  193 -- and column of a token within the file. `start_pos' gives the position of the
  194 -- start of the file and `eof_pos' a standard encoding for the end of file.
  195 -- `move_pos' calculates the new position after traversing a given character,
  196 -- assuming the usual eight character tab stops.
  197 
  198 #if defined(ALEX_POSN) || defined(ALEX_MONAD) || defined(ALEX_POSN_BYTESTRING) || defined(ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING) || defined(ALEX_GSCAN)
  199 data AlexPosn = AlexPn !Int !Int !Int
  200         deriving (Eq, Show, Ord)
  201 
  202 alexStartPos :: AlexPosn
  203 alexStartPos = AlexPn 0 1 1
  204 
  205 alexMove :: AlexPosn -> Char -> AlexPosn
  206 alexMove (AlexPn a l c) '\t' = AlexPn (a+1)  l     (c+alex_tab_size-((c-1) `mod` alex_tab_size))
  207 alexMove (AlexPn a l _) '\n' = AlexPn (a+1) (l+1)   1
  208 alexMove (AlexPn a l c) _    = AlexPn (a+1)  l     (c+1)
  209 #endif
  210 
  211 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  212 -- Monad (default and with ByteString input)
  213 
  214 #if defined(ALEX_MONAD) || defined(ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING)
  215 data AlexState = AlexState {
  216         alex_pos :: !AlexPosn,  -- position at current input location
  217 #ifndef ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING
  218         alex_inp :: String,     -- the current input
  219         alex_chr :: !Char,      -- the character before the input
  220         alex_bytes :: [Byte],
  221 #else /* ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING */
  222         alex_bpos:: !Int64,     -- bytes consumed so far
  223         alex_inp :: ByteString.ByteString,      -- the current input
  224         alex_chr :: !Char,      -- the character before the input
  225 #endif /* ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING */
  226         alex_scd :: !Int        -- the current startcode
  227 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_USER_STATE
  228       , alex_ust :: AlexUserState -- AlexUserState will be defined in the user program
  229 #endif
  230     }
  231 
  232 -- Compile with -funbox-strict-fields for best results!
  233 
  234 #ifndef ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING
  235 runAlex :: String -> Alex a -> Either String a
  236 runAlex input__ (Alex f)
  237    = case f (AlexState {alex_bytes = [],
  238 #else /* ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING */
  239 runAlex :: ByteString.ByteString -> Alex a -> Either String a
  240 runAlex input__ (Alex f)
  241    = case f (AlexState {alex_bpos = 0,
  242 #endif /* ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING */
  243                         alex_pos = alexStartPos,
  244                         alex_inp = input__,
  245                         alex_chr = '\n',
  246 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_USER_STATE
  247                         alex_ust = alexInitUserState,
  248 #endif
  249                         alex_scd = 0}) of Left msg -> Left msg
  250                                           Right ( _, a ) -> Right a
  251 
  252 newtype Alex a = Alex { unAlex :: AlexState -> Either String (AlexState, a) }
  253 
  254 instance Functor Alex where
  255   fmap f a = Alex $ \s -> case unAlex a s of
  256                             Left msg -> Left msg
  257                             Right (s', a') -> Right (s', f a')
  258 
  259 instance Applicative Alex where
  260   pure a   = Alex $ \s -> Right (s, a)
  261   fa <*> a = Alex $ \s -> case unAlex fa s of
  262                             Left msg -> Left msg
  263                             Right (s', f) -> case unAlex a s' of
  264                                                Left msg -> Left msg
  265                                                Right (s'', b) -> Right (s'', f b)
  266 
  267 instance Monad Alex where
  268   m >>= k  = Alex $ \s -> case unAlex m s of
  269                                 Left msg -> Left msg
  270                                 Right (s',a) -> unAlex (k a) s'
  271   return = App.pure
  272 
  273 alexGetInput :: Alex AlexInput
  274 alexGetInput
  275 #ifndef ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING
  276  = Alex $ \s@AlexState{alex_pos=pos,alex_chr=c,alex_bytes=bs,alex_inp=inp__} ->
  277         Right (s, (pos,c,bs,inp__))
  278 #else /* ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING */
  279  = Alex $ \s@AlexState{alex_pos=pos,alex_bpos=bpos,alex_chr=c,alex_inp=inp__} ->
  280         Right (s, (pos,c,inp__,bpos))
  281 #endif /* ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING */
  282 
  283 alexSetInput :: AlexInput -> Alex ()
  284 #ifndef ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING
  285 alexSetInput (pos,c,bs,inp__)
  286  = Alex $ \s -> case s{alex_pos=pos,alex_chr=c,alex_bytes=bs,alex_inp=inp__} of
  287 #else /* ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING */
  288 alexSetInput (pos,c,inp__,bpos)
  289  = Alex $ \s -> case s{alex_pos=pos,
  290                        alex_bpos=bpos,
  291                        alex_chr=c,
  292                        alex_inp=inp__} of
  293 #endif /* ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING */
  294                   state__@(AlexState{}) -> Right (state__, ())
  295 
  296 alexError :: String -> Alex a
  297 alexError message = Alex $ const $ Left message
  298 
  299 alexGetStartCode :: Alex Int
  300 alexGetStartCode = Alex $ \s@AlexState{alex_scd=sc} -> Right (s, sc)
  301 
  302 alexSetStartCode :: Int -> Alex ()
  303 alexSetStartCode sc = Alex $ \s -> Right (s{alex_scd=sc}, ())
  304 
  305 #if !defined(ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING) && defined(ALEX_MONAD_USER_STATE)
  306 alexGetUserState :: Alex AlexUserState
  307 alexGetUserState = Alex $ \s@AlexState{alex_ust=ust} -> Right (s,ust)
  308 
  309 alexSetUserState :: AlexUserState -> Alex ()
  310 alexSetUserState ss = Alex $ \s -> Right (s{alex_ust=ss}, ())
  311 #endif /* !defined(ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING) && defined(ALEX_MONAD_USER_STATE) */
  312 
  313 alexMonadScan = do
  314 #ifndef ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING
  315   inp__ <- alexGetInput
  316 #else /* ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING */
  317   inp__@(_,_,_,n) <- alexGetInput
  318 #endif /* ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING */
  319   sc <- alexGetStartCode
  320   case alexScan inp__ sc of
  321     AlexEOF -> alexEOF
  322     AlexError ((AlexPn _ line column),_,_,_) -> alexError $ "lexical error at line " ++ (show line) ++ ", column " ++ (show column)
  323     AlexSkip  inp__' _len -> do
  324         alexSetInput inp__'
  325         alexMonadScan
  326 #ifndef ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING
  327     AlexToken inp__' len action -> do
  328 #else /* ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING */
  329     AlexToken inp__'@(_,_,_,n') _ action -> let len = n'-n in do
  330 #endif /* ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING */
  331         alexSetInput inp__'
  332         action (ignorePendingBytes inp__) len
  333 
  334 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  335 -- Useful token actions
  336 
  337 #ifndef ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING
  338 type AlexAction result = AlexInput -> Int -> Alex result
  339 #else /* ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING */
  340 type AlexAction result = AlexInput -> Int64 -> Alex result
  341 #endif /* ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING */
  342 
  343 -- just ignore this token and scan another one
  344 -- skip :: AlexAction result
  345 skip _input _len = alexMonadScan
  346 
  347 -- ignore this token, but set the start code to a new value
  348 -- begin :: Int -> AlexAction result
  349 begin code _input _len = do alexSetStartCode code; alexMonadScan
  350 
  351 -- perform an action for this token, and set the start code to a new value
  352 andBegin :: AlexAction result -> Int -> AlexAction result
  353 (action `andBegin` code) input__ len = do
  354   alexSetStartCode code
  355   action input__ len
  356 
  357 #ifndef ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING
  358 token :: (AlexInput -> Int -> token) -> AlexAction token
  359 #else /* ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING */
  360 token :: (AlexInput -> Int64 -> token) -> AlexAction token
  361 #endif /* ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING */
  362 token t input__ len = return (t input__ len)
  363 #endif /* defined(ALEX_MONAD) || defined(ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING) */
  364 
  365 
  366 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  367 -- Basic wrapper
  368 
  369 #ifdef ALEX_BASIC
  370 type AlexInput = (Char,[Byte],String)
  371 
  372 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
  373 alexInputPrevChar (c,_,_) = c
  374 
  375 -- alexScanTokens :: String -> [token]
  376 alexScanTokens str = go ('\n',[],str)
  377   where go inp__@(_,_bs,s) =
  378           case alexScan inp__ 0 of
  379                 AlexEOF -> []
  380                 AlexError _ -> error "lexical error"
  381                 AlexSkip  inp__' _ln     -> go inp__'
  382                 AlexToken inp__' len act -> act (take len s) : go inp__'
  383 
  384 alexGetByte :: AlexInput -> Maybe (Byte,AlexInput)
  385 alexGetByte (c,(b:bs),s) = Just (b,(c,bs,s))
  386 alexGetByte (_,[],[])    = Nothing
  387 alexGetByte (_,[],(c:s)) = case utf8Encode' c of
  388                              (b, bs) -> Just (b, (c, bs, s))
  389 #endif
  390

  392 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  393 -- Basic wrapper, ByteString version
  394 
  395 #ifdef ALEX_BASIC_BYTESTRING
  396 
  397 -- alexScanTokens :: ByteString.ByteString -> [token]
  398 alexScanTokens str = go (AlexInput '\n' str 0)
  399   where go inp__ =
  400           case alexScan inp__ 0 of
  401                 AlexEOF -> []
  402                 AlexError _ -> error "lexical error"
  403                 AlexSkip  inp__' _len  -> go inp__'
  404                 AlexToken inp__' _ act ->
  405                   let len = alexBytePos inp__' - alexBytePos inp__ in
  406                   act (ByteString.take len (alexStr inp__)) : go inp__'
  407 
  408 #endif
  409 
  410 #ifdef ALEX_STRICT_BYTESTRING
  411 
  412 -- alexScanTokens :: ByteString.ByteString -> [token]
  413 alexScanTokens str = go (AlexInput '\n' str 0)
  414   where go inp__ =
  415           case alexScan inp__ 0 of
  416                 AlexEOF -> []
  417                 AlexError _ -> error "lexical error"
  418                 AlexSkip  inp__' _len  -> go inp__'
  419                 AlexToken inp__' _ act ->
  420                   let len = alexBytePos inp__' - alexBytePos inp__ in
  421                   act (ByteString.take len (alexStr inp__)) : go inp__'
  422 
  423 #endif

  426 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  427 -- Posn wrapper
  428 
  429 -- Adds text positions to the basic model.
  430 
  431 #ifdef ALEX_POSN
  432 --alexScanTokens :: String -> [token]
  433 alexScanTokens str0 = go (alexStartPos,'\n',[],str0)
  434   where go inp__@(pos,_,_,str) =
  435           case alexScan inp__ 0 of
  436                 AlexEOF -> []
  437                 AlexError ((AlexPn _ line column),_,_,_) -> error $ "lexical error at line " ++ (show line) ++ ", column " ++ (show column)
  438                 AlexSkip  inp__' _ln     -> go inp__'
  439                 AlexToken inp__' len act -> act pos (take len str) : go inp__'
  440 #endif
  441 
  442 
  443 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  444 -- Posn wrapper, ByteString version
  445 
  446 #ifdef ALEX_POSN_BYTESTRING
  447 --alexScanTokens :: ByteString.ByteString -> [token]
  448 alexScanTokens str0 = go (alexStartPos,'\n',str0,0)
  449   where go inp__@(pos,_,str,n) =
  450           case alexScan inp__ 0 of
  451                 AlexEOF -> []
  452                 AlexError ((AlexPn _ line column),_,_,_) -> error $ "lexical error at line " ++ (show line) ++ ", column " ++ (show column)
  453                 AlexSkip  inp__' _len       -> go inp__'
  454                 AlexToken inp__'@(_,_,_,n') _ act ->
  455                   act pos (ByteString.take (n'-n) str) : go inp__'
  456 #endif

  459 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  460 -- GScan wrapper
  461 
  462 -- For compatibility with previous versions of Alex, and because we can.
  463 
  464 #ifdef ALEX_GSCAN
  465 alexGScan stop__ state__ inp__ =
  466   alex_gscan stop__ alexStartPos '\n' [] inp__ (0,state__)
  467 
  468 alex_gscan stop__ p c bs inp__ (sc,state__) =
  469   case alexScan (p,c,bs,inp__) sc of
  470         AlexEOF     -> stop__ p c inp__ (sc,state__)
  471         AlexError _ -> stop__ p c inp__ (sc,state__)
  472         AlexSkip (p',c',bs',inp__') _len ->
  473           alex_gscan stop__ p' c' bs' inp__' (sc,state__)
  474         AlexToken (p',c',bs',inp__') len k ->
  475            k p c inp__ len (\scs -> alex_gscan stop__ p' c' bs' inp__' scs)                  (sc,state__)
  476 #endif
  477 alex_tab_size :: Int
  478 alex_tab_size = 8
  479 alex_base :: AlexAddr

  736 inChar,inComment,inString :: Int
  737 inChar = 1
  738 inComment = 2
  739 inString = 3
  740 alex_action_2 = enterComment `andBegin` inComment
  741 alex_action_3 = exitComment
  742 alex_action_5 = enterString `andBegin` inString
  743 alex_action_6 = addToString '\\'
  744 alex_action_7 = addToString '\n'
  745 alex_action_8 = addToString '\t'
  746 alex_action_9 = addToString '\''
  747 alex_action_10 = addToString '"'
  748 alex_action_11 = exitString
  749 alex_action_12 = addCurrentToString
  750 alex_action_13 = enterChar `andBegin` inChar
  751 alex_action_14 = addToChar '\\'
  752 alex_action_15 = addToChar '\n'
  753 alex_action_16 = addToChar '\t'
  754 alex_action_17 = addToChar '\''
  755 alex_action_18 = addToChar '"'
  756 alex_action_19 = exitChar
  757 alex_action_20 = addCurrentToChar
  758 alex_action_21 = scannerError $ \_ -> "invalid escape sequence"
  759 alex_action_22 = stringToken IntLiteral
  760 alex_action_23 = stringToken BooleanLiteral
  761 alex_action_24 = stringToken Keyword
  762 alex_action_25 = stringToken Identifier
  763 alex_action_26 = plainToken AssignOp
  764 alex_action_27 = stringToken CompoundAssignOp
  765 alex_action_28 = stringToken IncrementOp
  766 alex_action_29 = stringToken ArithmeticOp
  767 alex_action_30 = stringToken RelationOp
  768 alex_action_31 = stringToken EquationOp
  769 alex_action_32 = stringToken ConditionOp
  770 alex_action_33 = plainToken LCurly
  771 alex_action_34 = plainToken RCurly
  772 alex_action_35 = plainToken LParen
  773 alex_action_36 = plainToken RParen
  774 alex_action_37 = plainToken LBrack
  775 alex_action_38 = plainToken RBrack
  776 alex_action_39 = plainToken Choice
  777 alex_action_40 = plainToken Colon
  778 alex_action_41 = plainToken Semicolon
  779 alex_action_42 = plainToken Comma
  780 alex_action_43 = plainToken Negate
  781 alex_action_44 = scannerError $ \s -> BS.concat ["invalid character: ", s]
  782 
  783 #define ALEX_GHC 1

  790 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  791 -- INTERNALS and main scanner engine
  792 
  793 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
  794 #  define ILIT(n) n#
  795 #  define IBOX(n) (I# (n))
  796 #  define FAST_INT Int#
  797 -- Do not remove this comment. Required to fix CPP parsing when using GCC and a clang-compiled alex.
  798 #  if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ > 706
  799 #    define GTE(n,m) (tagToEnum# (n >=# m))
  800 #    define EQ(n,m) (tagToEnum# (n ==# m))
  801 #  else
  802 #    define GTE(n,m) (n >=# m)
  803 #    define EQ(n,m) (n ==# m)
  804 #  endif
  805 #  define PLUS(n,m) (n +# m)
  806 #  define MINUS(n,m) (n -# m)
  807 #  define TIMES(n,m) (n *# m)
  808 #  define NEGATE(n) (negateInt# (n))
  809 #  define IF_GHC(x) (x)
  810 #else
  811 #  define ILIT(n) (n)
  812 #  define IBOX(n) (n)
  813 #  define FAST_INT Int
  814 #  define GTE(n,m) (n >= m)
  815 #  define EQ(n,m) (n == m)
  816 #  define PLUS(n,m) (n + m)
  817 #  define MINUS(n,m) (n - m)
  818 #  define TIMES(n,m) (n * m)
  819 #  define NEGATE(n) (negate (n))
  820 #  define IF_GHC(x)
  821 #endif
  822 
  823 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
  824 data AlexAddr = AlexA# Addr#
  825 -- Do not remove this comment. Required to fix CPP parsing when using GCC and a clang-compiled alex.
  826 #if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ < 503
  827 uncheckedShiftL# = shiftL#
  828 #endif
  829 
  830 {-# INLINE alexIndexInt16OffAddr #-}
  831 alexIndexInt16OffAddr :: AlexAddr -> Int# -> Int#
  832 alexIndexInt16OffAddr (AlexA# arr) off =
  833 #ifdef WORDS_BIGENDIAN
  834   narrow16Int# i
  835   where
  836         i    = word2Int# ((high `uncheckedShiftL#` 8#) `or#` low)
  837         high = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 1#)))
  838         low  = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr off'))
  839         off' = off *# 2#
  840 #else
  841 #if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ >= 901
  842   int16ToInt#
  843 #endif
  844     (indexInt16OffAddr# arr off)
  845 #endif
  846 #else
  847 alexIndexInt16OffAddr arr off = arr ! off
  848 #endif
  849 
  850 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
  851 {-# INLINE alexIndexInt32OffAddr #-}
  852 alexIndexInt32OffAddr :: AlexAddr -> Int# -> Int#
  853 alexIndexInt32OffAddr (AlexA# arr) off =
  854 #ifdef WORDS_BIGENDIAN
  855   narrow32Int# i
  856   where
  857    i    = word2Int# ((b3 `uncheckedShiftL#` 24#) `or#`
  858                      (b2 `uncheckedShiftL#` 16#) `or#`
  859                      (b1 `uncheckedShiftL#` 8#) `or#` b0)
  860    b3   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 3#)))
  861    b2   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 2#)))
  862    b1   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 1#)))
  863    b0   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr off'))
  864    off' = off *# 4#
  865 #else
  866 #if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ >= 901
  867   int32ToInt#
  868 #endif
  869     (indexInt32OffAddr# arr off)
  870 #endif
  871 #else
  872 alexIndexInt32OffAddr arr off = arr ! off
  873 #endif
  874 
  875 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
  876 
  877 #if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ < 503
  878 quickIndex arr i = arr ! i
  879 #else
  880 -- GHC >= 503, unsafeAt is available from Data.Array.Base.
  881 quickIndex = unsafeAt
  882 #endif
  883 #else
  884 quickIndex arr i = arr ! i
  885 #endif
  886 
  887 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  888 -- Main lexing routines
  889 
  890 data AlexReturn a
  891   = AlexEOF
  892   | AlexError  !AlexInput
  893   | AlexSkip   !AlexInput !Int
  894   | AlexToken  !AlexInput !Int a
  895 
  896 -- alexScan :: AlexInput -> StartCode -> AlexReturn a
  897 alexScan input__ IBOX(sc)
  898   = alexScanUser undefined input__ IBOX(sc)
  899 
  900 alexScanUser user__ input__ IBOX(sc)
  901   = case alex_scan_tkn user__ input__ ILIT(0) input__ sc AlexNone of
  902   (AlexNone, input__') ->
  903     case alexGetByte input__ of
  904       Nothing ->
  905 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  906                                    trace ("End of input.") $
  907 #endif
  908                                    AlexEOF
  909       Just _ ->
  910 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  911                                    trace ("Error.") $
  912 #endif
  913                                    AlexError input__'
  914 
  915   (AlexLastSkip input__'' len, _) ->
  916 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  917     trace ("Skipping.") $
  918 #endif
  919     AlexSkip input__'' len
  920 
  921   (AlexLastAcc k input__''' len, _) ->
  922 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  923     trace ("Accept.") $
  924 #endif
  925     AlexToken input__''' len (alex_actions ! k)
  926 
  927 
  928 -- Push the input through the DFA, remembering the most recent accepting
  929 -- state it encountered.
  930 
  931 alex_scan_tkn user__ orig_input len input__ s last_acc =
  932   input__ `seq` -- strict in the input
  933   let
  934   new_acc = (check_accs (alex_accept `quickIndex` IBOX(s)))
  935   in
  936   new_acc `seq`
  937   case alexGetByte input__ of
  938      Nothing -> (new_acc, input__)
  939      Just (c, new_input) ->
  940 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  941       trace ("State: " ++ show IBOX(s) ++ ", char: " ++ show c) $
  942 #endif
  943       case fromIntegral c of { IBOX(ord_c) ->
  944         let
  945                 base   = alexIndexInt32OffAddr alex_base s
  946                 offset = PLUS(base,ord_c)
  947 
  948                 new_s = if GTE(offset,ILIT(0))
  949                           && let check  = alexIndexInt16OffAddr alex_check offset
  950                              in  EQ(check,ord_c)
  951                           then alexIndexInt16OffAddr alex_table offset
  952                           else alexIndexInt16OffAddr alex_deflt s
  953         in
  954         case new_s of
  955             ILIT(-1) -> (new_acc, input__)
  956                 -- on an error, we want to keep the input *before* the
  957                 -- character that failed, not after.
  958             _ -> alex_scan_tkn user__ orig_input
  959 #ifdef ALEX_LATIN1
  960                    PLUS(len,ILIT(1))
  961                    -- issue 119: in the latin1 encoding, *each* byte is one character
  962 #else
  963                    (if c < 0x80 || c >= 0xC0 then PLUS(len,ILIT(1)) else len)
  964                    -- note that the length is increased ONLY if this is the 1st byte in a char encoding)
  965 #endif
  966                    new_input new_s new_acc
  967       }
  968   where
  969         check_accs (AlexAccNone) = last_acc
  970         check_accs (AlexAcc a  ) = AlexLastAcc a input__ IBOX(len)
  971         check_accs (AlexAccSkip) = AlexLastSkip  input__ IBOX(len)
  972 #ifndef ALEX_NOPRED
  973         check_accs (AlexAccPred a predx rest)
  974            | predx user__ orig_input IBOX(len) input__
  975            = AlexLastAcc a input__ IBOX(len)
  976            | otherwise
  977            = check_accs rest
  978         check_accs (AlexAccSkipPred predx rest)
  979            | predx user__ orig_input IBOX(len) input__
  980            = AlexLastSkip input__ IBOX(len)
  981            | otherwise
  982            = check_accs rest
  983 #endif
  984 
  985 data AlexLastAcc
  986   = AlexNone
  987   | AlexLastAcc !Int !AlexInput !Int
  988   | AlexLastSkip     !AlexInput !Int
  989 
  990 data AlexAcc user
  991   = AlexAccNone
  992   | AlexAcc Int
  993   | AlexAccSkip
  994 #ifndef ALEX_NOPRED
  995   | AlexAccPred Int (AlexAccPred user) (AlexAcc user)
  996   | AlexAccSkipPred (AlexAccPred user) (AlexAcc user)
  997 
  998 type AlexAccPred user = user -> AlexInput -> Int -> AlexInput -> Bool
  999 
 1000 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1001 -- Predicates on a rule
 1002 
 1003 alexAndPred p1 p2 user__ in1 len in2
 1004   = p1 user__ in1 len in2 && p2 user__ in1 len in2
 1005 
 1006 --alexPrevCharIsPred :: Char -> AlexAccPred _
 1007 alexPrevCharIs c _ input__ _ _ = c == alexInputPrevChar input__
 1008 
 1009 alexPrevCharMatches f _ input__ _ _ = f (alexInputPrevChar input__)
 1010 
 1011 --alexPrevCharIsOneOfPred :: Array Char Bool -> AlexAccPred _
 1012 alexPrevCharIsOneOf arr _ input__ _ _ = arr ! alexInputPrevChar input__
 1013 
 1014 --alexRightContext :: Int -> AlexAccPred _
 1015 alexRightContext IBOX(sc) user__ _ _ input__ =
 1016      case alex_scan_tkn user__ input__ ILIT(0) input__ sc AlexNone of
 1017           (AlexNone, _) -> False
 1018           _ -> True
 1019         -- TODO: there's no need to find the longest
 1020         -- match when checking the right context, just
 1021         -- the first match will do.
 1022 #endif
 1023 {-# LINE 136 "src/Lexer/Lex.x" #-}
 1024 ---------------------------- Alex interface -----------------------------
 1025 -- The below code will be generated by the alex wrapper. They are put here for references.
 1026 {-
 1027 data AlexPosn = AlexPn !Int  -- absolute character offset
 1028                        !Int  -- line number
 1029                        !Int  -- column number
 1030 
 1031 type AlexInput = (AlexPosn,   -- current position,
 1032                   Char,       -- previous char
 1033                   ByteString.ByteString -- current input string
 1034                   Int64)      -- bytes consumed so far
 1035 
 1036 data AlexState = AlexState {
 1037         alex_pos :: !AlexPosn,  -- position at current input location
 1038         alex_inp :: ByteString.ByteString, -- the current input
 1039         alex_chr :: !Char,      -- the character before the input
 1040         alex_scd :: !Int,       -- the current startcode
 1041         alex_ust :: AlexUserState -- AlexUserState will be defined in the user program
 1042     }
 1043 
 1044 newtype Alex a = Alex { unAlex :: AlexState
 1045                                -> Either String (AlexState, a) }
 1046 
 1047 runAlex          :: ByteString.ByteString -> Alex a -> Either String a
 1048 
 1049 alexError        :: String -> Alex a
 1050 
 1051 alexMonadScan    :: Alex a
 1052 
 1053 -- token :: (ByteString.ByteString -> Int -> token) -> AlexAction token
 1054 -}
 1055 
 1056 
 1057 ---------------------------- Helper functions for scanning -----------------------------
 1058 
 1059 -- UserState to track comment depth and value of string literal
 1060 data AlexUserState = AlexUserState { lexerCommentDepth :: Int
 1061                                    , lexerStringState :: Bool
 1062                                    , lexerCharState :: Bool
 1063                                    , lexerStringValue :: ByteString
 1064                                    , errors :: [CompileError]
 1065                                    }
 1066 
 1067 alexInitUserState :: AlexUserState
 1068 alexInitUserState = AlexUserState { lexerCommentDepth = 0
 1069                                   , lexerStringState = False
 1070                                   , lexerCharState = False
 1071                                   , lexerStringValue = ""
 1072                                   , errors = []
 1073                                   }
 1074 
 1075 posnFromAlex :: AlexPosn -> SL.Posn
 1076 posnFromAlex (AlexPn offset row col) = SL.Posn offset (row-1) (col-1)
 1077 
 1078 locatedAt :: AlexPosn -> AlexPosn -> a -> SL.Located a
 1079 locatedAt start stop = SL.LocatedAt (SL.Range (posnFromAlex start) (posnFromAlex stop))
 1080 
 1081 getAlexState :: Alex AlexState
 1082 getAlexState = Alex $ \s -> Right(s, s)
 1083 
 1084 alexEOF :: Alex (SL.Located Token)
 1085 alexEOF = Alex $ \s@AlexState{alex_pos=pos} -> Right(s, locatedAt pos pos EOF)
 1086 
 1087 getLexerCommentDepth :: Alex Int
 1088 getLexerCommentDepth = Alex $ \s@AlexState{alex_ust=ust} -> Right (s, lexerCommentDepth ust)
 1089 
 1090 setLexerCommentDepth :: Int -> Alex ()
 1091 setLexerCommentDepth depth = Alex $ \s -> Right (s { alex_ust=(alex_ust s) {lexerCommentDepth=depth} }, ())
 1092 
 1093 getLexerStringValue :: Alex ByteString
 1094 getLexerStringValue = Alex $ \s@AlexState{alex_ust=ust} -> Right (s, lexerStringValue ust)
 1095 
 1096 setLexerStringValue :: ByteString -> Alex ()
 1097 setLexerStringValue value = Alex $ \s -> Right (s { alex_ust=(alex_ust s) {lexerStringValue=value} }, ())
 1098 
 1099 getLexerStringState :: Alex Bool
 1100 getLexerStringState = Alex $ \s@AlexState{alex_ust=ust} -> Right (s, lexerStringState ust)
 1101 
 1102 setLexerStringState :: Bool -> Alex ()
 1103 setLexerStringState state = Alex $ \s -> Right (s { alex_ust=(alex_ust s) {lexerStringState=state} }, ())
 1104 
 1105 getLexerCharState :: Alex Bool
 1106 getLexerCharState = Alex $ \s@AlexState{alex_ust=ust} -> Right (s, lexerCharState ust)
 1107 
 1108 setLexerCharState :: Bool -> Alex ()
 1109 setLexerCharState state = Alex $ \s -> Right (s { alex_ust=(alex_ust s) {lexerCharState=state} }, ())
 1110 
 1111 addError :: CompileError -> Alex ()
 1112 addError error = Alex $ \s@AlexState{alex_ust=(AlexUserState{errors=errors})} -> Right(s{alex_ust=(alex_ust s) {errors=errors++[error]}}, ())
 1113 
 1114 getTokenStop :: AlexPosn -> ByteString -> AlexPosn
 1115 getTokenStop posn inp = Text.foldl' alexMove posn $ Enc.decodeUtf8 $ BS.toStrict inp
 1116 
 1117 ----- Scanning functions ------
 1118 
 1119 type Action = AlexInput -> Int64 -> Alex (SL.Located Token)
 1120 
 1121 stringToken :: (Text -> Token) -> Action
 1122 stringToken tok (start, _, inp, _) len =
 1123   let content = BS.take len inp
 1124       stop = getTokenStop start content
 1125   in return $ locatedAt start stop $ tok $ Enc.decodeUtf8 $ BS.toStrict content
 1126 
 1127 plainToken :: Token -> Action
 1128 plainToken tok (start, _, inp, _) len =
 1129   let stop = getTokenStop start $ BS.take len inp
 1130   in return $ locatedAt start stop tok
 1131 
 1132 enterComment :: Action
 1133 enterComment inp len =
 1134     do cd <- getLexerCommentDepth
 1135        setLexerCommentDepth (cd + 1)
 1136        skip inp len
 1137 
 1138 exitComment :: Action
 1139 exitComment inp len =
 1140     do cd <- getLexerCommentDepth
 1141        setLexerCommentDepth (cd - 1)
 1142        when (cd == 1) (alexSetStartCode 0)
 1143        skip inp len
 1144 
 1145 enterString :: Action
 1146 enterString inp len =
 1147     do setLexerStringState True
 1148        setLexerStringValue ""
 1149        skip inp len
 1150 
 1151 exitString :: Action
 1152 exitString (pos, _, _, _) len =
 1153     do value <- getLexerStringValue
 1154        setLexerStringState False
 1155        alexSetStartCode 0
 1156        return $ locatedAt pos pos (StringLiteral $ Enc.decodeUtf8 $ BS.toStrict $ BS.reverse value)
 1157 
 1158 addToString :: Char -> Action
 1159 addToString c inp len =
 1160     do value <- getLexerStringValue
 1161        setLexerStringValue $ C8.cons c value
 1162        skip inp len
 1163 
 1164 addCurrentToString :: Action
 1165 addCurrentToString inp@(_, _, str, _) len = addToString (C8.head str) inp len
 1166 
 1167 enterChar :: Action
 1168 enterChar inp len =
 1169     do setLexerCharState True
 1170        setLexerStringValue ""
 1171        skip inp len
 1172 
 1173 exitChar :: Action
 1174 exitChar (pos, _, _, _) len =
 1175     do value <- getLexerStringValue
 1176        setLexerCharState False
 1177        alexSetStartCode 0
 1178        return $ locatedAt pos pos (CharLiteral $ Enc.decodeUtf8 $ BS.toStrict value)
 1179 
 1180 addToChar :: Char -> Action
 1181 addToChar c inp len =
 1182     do value <- getLexerStringValue
 1183        if (BS.length value > 0)
 1184           then scannerError (\_ -> "character literal not closed") inp len
 1185           else do setLexerStringValue $ C8.pack [c]
 1186                   skip inp len
 1187 
 1188 addCurrentToChar :: Action
 1189 addCurrentToChar inp@(_, _, str, _) len = addToChar (C8.head str) inp len
 1190 
 1191 scannerError :: (ByteString -> ByteString) -> Action
 1192 scannerError fn inp@(start, _, text, _) len = do
 1193     let content = BS.take len text
 1194     let stop = getTokenStop start content
 1195     addError $ CompileError (Just $ SL.Range (posnFromAlex start) (posnFromAlex stop)) (Enc.decodeUtf8 $ BS.toStrict $ fn content)
 1196     skip inp len
